[(a*g+b*g*x)^(-2-m)*(c*i+d*i*x)^m*(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))^p,x,4,-exp(A*(1+m)/(B*n))*(a+b*x)*(g*(a+b*x))^(-2-m)*(i*(c+d*x))^(2+m)*(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n)^((1+m)/n)*GAMMA(1+p,(1+m)*(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))/(B*n))*(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))^p/((b*c-a*d)*i^2*(1+m)*(c+d*x)*((1+m)*(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))/(B*n))^p)],
[(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))^3/((a+b*x)*(c+d*x)),x,4,1/4*(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))^4/(B*(b*c-a*d)*n)],
[(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))^2/((a+b*x)*(c+d*x)),x,4,1/3*(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))^3/(B*(b*c-a*d)*n)],
[(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))/((a+b*x)*(c+d*x)),x,3,1/2*(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))^2/(B*(b*c-a*d)*n)],

[(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))^p/((a+b*x)*(c+d*x)),x,4,(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))^(1+p)/(B*(b*c-a*d)*n*(1+p))],

[1/((a+b*x)*(c+d*x)*(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))),x,4,log(A+B*log(e*(a+b*x)^n/(c+d*x)^n))/(B*(b*c-a*d)*n)],
